  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=7.3)
    The story successfully integrates its disparate elements into a cohesive whole that explores the theme of confronting fear. The imagery is often striking, and the narrative builds to a satisfying conclusion. However, some elements (particularly the garage sales timeframe) feel forced rather than organic to the story's development. Despite occasional lapses into overly ornate language, the story leaves the reader with the lingering impression of a personal triumph over fear, suggesting depth beyond the explicit narrative.
